 jieselvi aaj andhra pradesh ke sriharikota se 4:57 baje 450 karod rupee kii laagat se taiyaar hua vah sanchaar satellite antariksh main le jane vaala he, jise pradhanmantri narendra modi ne srilanka tathaa nepal sahit saat dakshin asian deshon ko tohfe main dene kii ghoshnaa kii he
 
 
 Pakistan has denied being part of it, not even as a beneficiary
 
 
 sriharikota main bhartiya antariksh anusandhan sanghathan, yani isro kaa control room udantashtaree ke aakaar main bana hua he, jisamen is vakt desh ke sarvshereshth antariksh vigyaani or ejeeniyar baithe hai, or ve satellite or use antariksh main le jane vaale rocket kii nas-nas par nazaren rakhenge
